## ï¿½xï¿½ï¿½ TRANSFORMACIï¿½ N DIGITAL COMPLETA CON IA



### **Framework de Transformaciï¿½ï¿½n Digital**

```python

class DigitalTransformationFramework:

    def __init__(self):

        self.phases = {

            'assessment': 'Evaluaciï¿½ï¿½n actual',

            'strategy': 'Estrategia de transformaciï¿½ï¿½n',

            'implementation': 'Implementaciï¿½ï¿½n',

            'optimization': 'Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n continua'

        }

        self.maturity_levels = {

            1: 'Inicial',

            2: 'En desarrollo',

            3: 'Definido',

            4: 'Gestionado',

            5: 'Optimizado'

        }

    

    def assess_current_state(self, organization_data):

        """Evaluar estado actual de la organizaciï¿½ï¿½n"""

        assessment = {

            'technology_maturity': self.assess_technology_maturity(organization_data),

            'data_maturity': self.assess_data_maturity(organization_data),

            'process_maturity': self.assess_process_maturity(organization_data),

            'culture_maturity': self.assess_culture_maturity(organization_data)

        }

        

        # Calcular score general

        overall_score = np.mean(list(assessment.values()))

        assessment['overall_maturity'] = overall_score

        assessment['maturity_level'] = self.maturity_levels[int(overall_score)]

        

        return assessment

    

    def assess_technology_maturity(self, data):

        """Evaluar madurez tecnolï¿½ï¿½gica"""

        tech_indicators = [

            data.get('cloud_adoption', 0),

            data.get('ai_tools_usage', 0),

            data.get('automation_level', 0),

            data.get('integration_level', 0)

        ]

        return np.mean(tech_indicators)

    

    def assess_data_maturity(self, data):

        """Evaluar madurez de datos"""

        data_indicators = [

            data.get('data_quality', 0),

            data.get('data_governance', 0),

            data.get('analytics_capability', 0),

            data.get('data_driven_decisions', 0)

        ]

        return np.mean(data_indicators)

    

    def assess_process_maturity(self, data):

        """Evaluar madurez de procesos"""

        process_indicators = [

            data.get('process_automation', 0),

            data.get('workflow_optimization', 0),

            data.get('agile_methodology', 0),

            data.get('continuous_improvement', 0)

        ]

        return np.mean(process_indicators)

    

    def assess_culture_maturity(self, data):

        """Evaluar madurez cultural"""

        culture_indicators = [

            data.get('innovation_culture', 0),

            data.get('change_readiness', 0),

            data.get('digital_skills', 0),

            data.get('collaboration_tools', 0)

        ]

        return np.mean(culture_indicators)

    

    def create_transformation_roadmap(self, assessment):

        """Crear roadmap de transformaciï¿½ï¿½n"""

        roadmap = {

            'phase_1': self.plan_phase_1(assessment),

            'phase_2': self.plan_phase_2(assessment),

            'phase_3': self.plan_phase_3(assessment),

            'phase_4': self.plan_phase_4(assessment)

        }

        return roadmap

    

    def plan_phase_1(self, assessment):

        """Planificar fase 1: Fundaciï¿½ï¿½n"""

        if assessment['overall_maturity'] < 2:

            return {

                'duration': '3-6 meses',

                'objectives': [

                    'Establecer infraestructura bï¿½ï¿½sica',

                    'Implementar herramientas de datos',

                    'Capacitar al equipo bï¿½ï¿½sico',

                    'Crear procesos fundamentales'

                ],

                'deliverables': [

                    'Auditorï¿½ï¿½a completa',

                    'Plan de infraestructura',

                    'Programa de capacitaciï¿½ï¿½n',

                    'Procesos documentados'

                ]

            }

        return None

    

    def plan_phase_2(self, assessment):

        """Planificar fase 2: Desarrollo"""

        if 2 <= assessment['overall_maturity'] < 3:

            return {

                'duration': '6-12 meses',

                'objectives': [

                    'Implementar IA bï¿½ï¿½sica',

                    'Automatizar procesos clave',

                    'Mejorar calidad de datos',

                    'Desarrollar capacidades analï¿½ï¿½ticas'

                ],

                'deliverables': [

                    'Modelos de IA implementados',

                    'Procesos automatizados',

                    'Dashboard de mï¿½ï¿½tricas',

                    'Equipo capacitado'

                ]

            }

        return None

    

    def plan_phase_3(self, assessment):

        """Planificar fase 3: Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n"""

        if 3 <= assessment['overall_maturity'] < 4:

            return {

                'duration': '12-18 meses',

                'objectives': [

                    'IA avanzada y personalizaciï¿½ï¿½n',

                    'Integraciï¿½ï¿½n completa de sistemas',

                    'Cultura data-driven',

                    'Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n continua'

                ],

                'deliverables': [

                    'Sistema de IA integrado',

                    'Personalizaciï¿½ï¿½n avanzada',

                    'Cultura transformada',

                    'Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n sistemï¿½ï¿½tica'

                ]

            }

        return None

    

    def plan_phase_4(self, assessment):

        """Planificar fase 4: Liderazgo"""

        if assessment['overall_maturity'] >= 4:

            return {

                'duration': '18+ meses',

                'objectives': [

                    'Liderazgo en IA',

                    'Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n disruptiva',

                    'Ecosistema digital completo',

                    'Transformaciï¿½ï¿½n continua'

                ],

                'deliverables': [

                    'Liderazgo reconocido',

                    'Innovaciones disruptivas',

                    'Ecosistema maduro',

                    'Transformaciï¿½ï¿½n continua'

                ]

            }

        return None



# Uso del framework

transformation = DigitalTransformationFramework()

org_data = {

    'cloud_adoption': 3,

    'ai_tools_usage': 2,

    'automation_level': 2,

    'integration_level': 1,

    'data_quality': 3,

    'data_governance': 2,

    'analytics_capability': 2,

    'data_driven_decisions': 1,

    'process_automation': 2,

    'workflow_optimization': 2,

    'agile_methodology': 3,

    'continuous_improvement': 2,

    'innovation_culture': 2,

    'change_readiness': 2,

    'digital_skills': 2,

    'collaboration_tools': 3

}



assessment = transformation.assess_current_state(org_data)

roadmap = transformation.create_transformation_roadmap(assessment)

```

## ï¿½x ï¿½ LIDERAZGO EN IA MARKETING Y GESTIï¿½ N DE EQUIPOS



### **Framework de Liderazgo en IA**

```python

class AILeadershipFramework:

    def __init__(self):

        self.leadership_dimensions = {

            'vision': 'Visiï¿½ï¿½n estratï¿½ï¿½gica',

            'technical': 'Competencia tï¿½ï¿½cnica',

            'change': 'Gestiï¿½ï¿½n del cambio',

            'team': 'Desarrollo de equipos',

            'innovation': 'Fomento de la innovaciï¿½ï¿½n'

        }

        self.team_roles = {

            'ai_strategist': 'Estratega de IA',

            'data_scientist': 'Cientï¿½ï¿½fico de Datos',

            'ml_engineer': 'Ingeniero de ML',

            'marketing_analyst': 'Analista de Marketing',

            'product_manager': 'Product Manager',

            'ux_researcher': 'Investigador UX'

        }

    

    def assess_leadership_gaps(self, current_skills, required_skills):

        """Evaluar brechas de liderazgo"""

        gaps = {}

        for dimension, required_level in required_skills.items():

            current_level = current_skills.get(dimension, 0)

            gap = required_level - current_level

            if gap > 0:

                gaps[dimension] = {

                    'current': current_level,

                    'required': required_level,

                    'gap': gap,

                    'priority': 'high' if gap > 2 else 'medium' if gap > 1 else 'low'

                }

        return gaps

    

    def create_team_structure(self, organization_size, budget, complexity):

        """Crear estructura de equipo recomendada"""

        if organization_size < 50:

            return self.create_small_team_structure(budget, complexity)

        elif organization_size < 200:

            return self.create_medium_team_structure(budget, complexity)

        else:

            return self.create_large_team_structure(budget, complexity)

    

    def create_small_team_structure(self, budget, complexity):

        """Estructura para equipos pequeï¿½ï¿½os"""

        team = {

            'ai_marketing_manager': {

                'role': 'AI Marketing Manager',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Estrategia general de IA',

                    'Coordinaciï¿½ï¿½n de proyectos',

                    'Comunicaciï¿½ï¿½n con stakeholders'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['strategic_thinking', 'ai_basics', 'project_management']

            },

            'marketing_analyst': {

                'role': 'Marketing Analyst',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de datos',

                    'Implementaciï¿½ï¿½n de herramientas',

                    'Reportes y dashboards'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['data_analysis', 'marketing_knowledge', 'tool_usage']

            }

        }

        

        if complexity > 3:

            team['data_scientist'] = {

                'role': 'Data Scientist (Part-time)',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Modelos de ML',

                    'Anï¿½ï¿½lisis avanzado',

                    'Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de algoritmos'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['machine_learning', 'statistics', 'programming']

            }

        

        return team

    

    def create_medium_team_structure(self, budget, complexity):

        """Estructura para equipos medianos"""

        team = {

            'ai_marketing_director': {

                'role': 'AI Marketing Director',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Liderazgo estratï¿½ï¿½gico',

                    'Gestiï¿½ï¿½n de presupuesto',

                    'Relaciones externas'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['strategic_leadership', 'budget_management', 'stakeholder_management']

            },

            'ai_strategist': {

                'role': 'AI Strategist',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Roadmap de IA',

                    'Evaluaciï¿½ï¿½n de tecnologï¿½ï¿½as',

                    'Arquitectura de soluciones'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['ai_strategy', 'technology_evaluation', 'solution_architecture']

            },

            'data_science_team': {

                'role': 'Data Science Team (2-3 personas)',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Modelos de ML',

                    'Anï¿½ï¿½lisis predictivo',

                    'Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de algoritmos'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['machine_learning', 'deep_learning', 'statistics']

            },

            'marketing_analysts': {

                'role': 'Marketing Analysts (2-3 personas)',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de campaï¿½ï¿½as',

                    'Implementaciï¿½ï¿½n de IA',

                    'Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de procesos'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['marketing_analysis', 'ai_tools', 'process_optimization']

            }

        }

        

        return team

    

    def create_large_team_structure(self, budget, complexity):

        """Estructura para equipos grandes"""

        team = {

            'chief_ai_officer': {

                'role': 'Chief AI Officer',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Visiï¿½ï¿½n estratï¿½ï¿½gica de IA',

                    'Liderazgo ejecutivo',

                    'Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n organizacional'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['executive_leadership', 'ai_vision', 'organizational_innovation']

            },

            'ai_marketing_vp': {

                'role': 'VP AI Marketing',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Estrategia de IA marketing',

                    'Gestiï¿½ï¿½n de equipos',

                    'Presupuesto y recursos'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['vp_leadership', 'ai_marketing_strategy', 'team_management']

            },

            'ai_research_team': {

                'role': 'AI Research Team (5-8 personas)',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Investigaciï¿½ï¿½n de IA',

                    'Desarrollo de algoritmos',

                    'Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n tecnolï¿½ï¿½gica'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['ai_research', 'algorithm_development', 'innovation']

            },

            'data_science_team': {

                'role': 'Data Science Team (8-12 personas)',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Modelos de ML avanzados',

                    'Anï¿½ï¿½lisis predictivo',

                    'Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de sistemas'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['advanced_ml', 'predictive_analytics', 'system_optimization']

            },

            'marketing_ai_team': {

                'role': 'Marketing AI Team (6-10 personas)',

                'responsibilities': [

                    'Implementaciï¿½ï¿½n de IA',

                    'Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de campaï¿½ï¿½as',

                    'Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de performance'

                ],

                'skills_required': ['ai_implementation', 'campaign_optimization', 'performance_analysis']

            }

        }

        

        return team

    

    def create_development_plan(self, team_member, current_skills, target_role):

        """Crear plan de desarrollo individual"""

        development_plan = {

            'current_role': team_member['role'],

            'target_role': target_role,

            'skill_gaps': self.identify_skill_gaps(current_skills, target_role),

            'learning_path': self.create_learning_path(current_skills, target_role),

            'timeline': self.estimate_timeline(current_skills, target_role),

            'resources': self.recommend_resources(target_role)

        }

        

        return development_plan

    

    def identify_skill_gaps(self, current_skills, target_role):

        """Identificar brechas de habilidades"""

        role_requirements = {

            'ai_strategist': ['strategic_thinking', 'ai_knowledge', 'business_acumen'],

            'data_scientist': ['machine_learning', 'statistics', 'programming'],

            'ml_engineer': ['software_engineering', 'ml_ops', 'cloud_platforms'],

            'marketing_analyst': ['marketing_knowledge', 'data_analysis', 'tool_usage']

        }

        

        required_skills = role_requirements.get(target_role, [])

        gaps = [skill for skill in required_skills if skill not in current_skills]

        

        return gaps

    

    def create_learning_path(self, current_skills, target_role):

        """Crear ruta de aprendizaje"""

        learning_path = {

            'phase_1': {

                'duration': '1-2 meses',

                'focus': 'Fundamentos',

                'activities': [

                    'Cursos online bï¿½ï¿½sicos',

                    'Lectura de documentaciï¿½ï¿½n',

                    'Prï¿½ï¿½ctica con herramientas'

                ]

            },

            'phase_2': {

                'duration': '2-3 meses',

                'focus': 'Aplicaciï¿½ï¿½n prï¿½ï¿½ctica',

                'activities': [

                    'Proyectos prï¿½ï¿½cticos',

                    'Mentorï¿½ï¿½a con expertos',

                    'Certificaciones bï¿½ï¿½sicas'

                ]

            },

            'phase_3': {

                'duration': '3-6 meses',

                'focus': 'Especializaciï¿½ï¿½n',

                'activities': [

                    'Proyectos complejos',

                    'Certificaciones avanzadas',

                    'Contribuciï¿½ï¿½n a equipos'

                ]

            }

        }

        

        return learning_path



# Uso del framework de liderazgo

leadership = AILeadershipFramework()

current_skills = ['marketing_knowledge', 'basic_analytics']

team_structure = leadership.create_team_structure(100, 'medium', 4)

development_plan = leadership.create_development_plan(

    {'role': 'Marketing Analyst'}, 

    current_skills, 

    'ai_strategist'

)

```

## ï¿½x ` Mï¿½0 TRICAS DE ï¿½0 XITO DEL LIDERAZGO EN IA



### **KPIs de Liderazgo**

- **Adopciï¿½ï¿½n de IA:** % de equipos usando IA

- **ROI de Proyectos:** Retorno de inversiï¿½ï¿½n promedio

- **Satisfacciï¿½ï¿½n del Equipo:** NPS interno

- **Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n:** Nï¿½ï¿½mero de proyectos innovadores

- **Capacitaciï¿½ï¿½n:** Horas de entrenamiento por empleado

- **Retenciï¿½ï¿½n:** % de retenciï¿½ï¿½n del equipo de IA



### **Mï¿½ï¿½tricas de Transformaciï¿½ï¿½n**

- **Velocidad de Implementaciï¿½ï¿½n:** Tiempo promedio de proyectos

- **Calidad de Datos:** % de datos limpios y estructurados

- **Automatizaciï¿½ï¿½n:** % de procesos automatizados

- **Decisiones Data-Driven:** % de decisiones basadas en datos

- **Cultura Digital:** Score de madurez digital

- **Innovaciï¿½ï¿½n Continua:** Nï¿½ï¿½mero de mejoras implementadas

*Secciones: Deep Learning, Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de Competencia, Transformaciï¿½ï¿½n Digital, Liderazgo en IA*

## ï¿½xRï¿½ MARKETING GLOBAL Y ESTRATEGIAS INTERNACIONALES CON IA

### **Sistema de Localizaciï¿½ï¿½n Inteligente**
```python
import requests
from googletrans import Translator
import pandas as pd
from textblob import TextBlob
import numpy as np

class GlobalMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.translator = Translator()
        self.market_data = {}
        self.cultural_insights = {}
    
    def analyze_global_markets(self, markets):
        """Analizar mercados globales con IA"""
        analysis = {}
        
        for market in markets:
            market_analysis = {
                'market_size': self.get_market_size(market),
                'competition_level': self.analyze_competition(market),
                'cultural_factors': self.analyze_cultural_factors(market),
                'regulatory_environment': self.get_regulatory_info(market),
                'digital_adoption': self.analyze_digital_adoption(market),
                'ai_readiness': self.assess_ai_readiness(market)
            }
            analysis[market] = market_analysis
        
        return analysis
    
    def get_market_size(self, market):
        """Obtener tamaï¿½ï¿½o del mercado"""
        # Datos de ejemplo - en implementaciï¿½ï¿½n real usar APIs de datos econï¿½ï¿½micos
        market_sizes = {
            'US': {'gdp': 25000000, 'population': 331000000, 'digital_penetration': 0.95},
            'China': {'gdp': 18000000, 'population': 1400000000, 'digital_penetration': 0.85},
            'India': {'gdp': 3500000, 'population': 1380000000, 'digital_penetration': 0.65},
            'Brazil': {'gdp': 2000000, 'population': 215000000, 'digital_penetration': 0.80},
            'Germany': {'gdp': 4500000, 'population': 83000000, 'digital_penetration': 0.90}
        }
        return market_sizes.get(market, {})
    
    def analyze_cultural_factors(self, market):
        """Analizar factores culturales"""
        cultural_data = {
            'US': {'individualism': 0.9, 'uncertainty_avoidance': 0.4, 'power_distance': 0.3},
            'China': {'individualism': 0.2, 'uncertainty_avoidance': 0.6, 'power_distance': 0.8},
            'India': {'individualism': 0.3, 'uncertainty_avoidance': 0.5, 'power_distance': 0.7},
            'Brazil': {'individualism': 0.6, 'uncertainty_avoidance': 0.7, 'power_distance': 0.6},
            'Germany': {'individualism': 0.7, 'uncertainty_avoidance': 0.8, 'power_distance': 0.3}
        }
        return cultural_data.get(market, {})
    
    def localize_content(self, content, target_market, content_type='marketing'):
        """Localizar contenido para mercado especï¿½ï¿½fico"""
        # Traducciï¿½ï¿½n inteligente
        translated = self.translator.translate(content, dest=self.get_language_code(target_market))
        
        # Adaptaciï¿½ï¿½n cultural
        cultural_adaptation = self.adapt_cultural_content(translated.text, target_market, content_type)
        
        # Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n para el mercado
        optimized_content = self.optimize_for_market(cultural_adaptation, target_market)
        
        return {
            'original': content,
            'translated': translated.text,
            'culturally_adapted': cultural_adaptation,
            'optimized': optimized_content,
            'market': target_market
        }
    
    def adapt_cultural_content(self, content, market, content_type):
        """Adaptar contenido culturalmente"""
        cultural_rules = {
            'US': {
                'tone': 'direct',
                'formality': 'casual',
                'call_to_action': 'aggressive'
            },
            'China': {
                'tone': 'respectful',
                'formality': 'formal',
                'call_to_action': 'subtle'
            },
            'India': {
                'tone': 'warm',
                'formality': 'moderate',
                'call_to_action': 'encouraging'
            },
            'Brazil': {
                'tone': 'friendly',
                'formality': 'casual',
                'call_to_action': 'enthusiastic'
            },
            'Germany': {
                'tone': 'professional',
                'formality': 'formal',
                'call_to_action': 'clear'
            }
        }
        
        rules = cultural_rules.get(market, {})
        adapted_content = content
        
        # Aplicar reglas culturales
        if rules['tone'] == 'direct':
            adapted_content = self.make_direct(adapted_content)
        elif rules['tone'] == 'respectful':
            adapted_content = self.make_respectful(adapted_content)
        
        return adapted_content
    
    def optimize_for_market(self, content, market):
        """Optimizar contenido para el mercado especï¿½ï¿½fico"""
        # Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de sentimiento
        sentiment = TextBlob(content).sentiment
        
        # Ajustar segï¿½ï¿½n preferencias del mercado
        market_preferences = {
            'US': {'sentiment_threshold': 0.1, 'length_preference': 'medium'},
            'China': {'sentiment_threshold': 0.3, 'length_preference': 'long'},
            'India': {'sentiment_threshold': 0.2, 'length_preference': 'medium'},
            'Brazil': {'sentiment_threshold': 0.0, 'length_preference': 'short'},
            'Germany': {'sentiment_threshold': 0.1, 'length_preference': 'long'}
        }
        
        preferences = market_preferences.get(market, {})
        
        # Ajustar sentimiento si es necesario
        if sentiment.polarity < preferences.get('sentiment_threshold', 0):
            content = self.boost_sentiment(content)
        
        return content
    
    def create_global_campaign_strategy(self, markets, budget, objectives):
        """Crear estrategia de campaï¿½ï¿½a global"""
        strategy = {
            'budget_allocation': self.allocate_budget(markets, budget),
            'content_strategy': self.create_content_strategy(markets),
            'channel_strategy': self.create_channel_strategy(markets),
            'timeline': self.create_global_timeline(markets),
            'success_metrics': self.define_global_metrics(markets, objectives)
        }
        
        return strategy
    
    def allocate_budget(self, markets, total_budget):
        """Asignar presupuesto por mercado"""
        market_weights = {}
        
        for market in markets:
            market_analysis = self.analyze_global_markets([market])[market]
            
            # Calcular peso basado en mï¿½ï¿½ltiples factores
            weight = (
                market_analysis['market_size']['gdp'] * 0.4 +
                market_analysis['digital_adoption'] * 0.3 +
                market_analysis['ai_readiness'] * 0.3
            )
            market_weights[market] = weight
        
        # Normalizar pesos
        total_weight = sum(market_weights.values())
        budget_allocation = {}
        
        for market, weight in market_weights.items():
            budget_allocation[market] = (weight / total_weight) * total_budget
        
        return budget_allocation

# Uso del sistema global
global_marketing = GlobalMarketingAI()
markets = ['US', 'China', 'India', 'Brazil', 'Germany']
market_analysis = global_marketing.analyze_global_markets(markets)
strategy = global_marketing.create_global_campaign_strategy(markets, 1000000, ['awareness', 'conversion'])
```

## ï¿½x}ï¿½ CREATIVIDAD AVANZADA Y DISEï¿½ O CON IA

### **Sistema de Generaciï¿½ï¿½n Creativa**
```python
from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont
import requests
import json

class CreativeAIMarketing:
    def __init__(self):
        self.color_palettes = {}
        self.font_styles = {}
        self.layout_templates = {}
    
    def generate_visual_content(self, brief, style_preferences):
        """Generar contenido visual con IA"""
        content = {
            'images': self.generate_images(brief, style_preferences),
            'graphics': self.generate_graphics(brief, style_preferences),
            'layouts': self.generate_layouts(brief, style_preferences),
            'color_schemes': self.generate_color_schemes(brief, style_preferences)
        }
        return content
    
    def generate_images(self, brief, style_preferences):
        """Generar imï¿½ï¿½genes con IA"""
        # Integraciï¿½ï¿½n con DALL-E, Midjourney, o Stable Diffusion
        prompts = self.create_image_prompts(brief, style_preferences)
        
        generated_images = []
        for prompt in prompts:
            # Aquï¿½ï¿½ irï¿½ï¿½a la integraciï¿½ï¿½n real con APIs de generaciï¿½ï¿½n de imï¿½ï¿½genes
            image_data = {
                'prompt': prompt,
                'style': style_preferences.get('style', 'modern'),
                'mood': style_preferences.get('mood', 'professional'),
                'colors': style_preferences.get('colors', 'vibrant')
            }
            generated_images.append(image_data)
        
        return generated_images
    
    def create_image_prompts(self, brief, style_preferences):
        """Crear prompts optimizados para generaciï¿½ï¿½n de imï¿½ï¿½genes"""
        base_prompt = brief.get('description', '')
        style = style_preferences.get('style', 'modern')
        mood = style_preferences.get('mood', 'professional')
        
        style_modifiers = {
            'modern': 'clean, minimalist, contemporary design',
            'vintage': 'retro, classic, nostalgic aesthetic',
            'futuristic': 'sleek, high-tech, innovative design',
            'minimalist': 'simple, clean, uncluttered composition',
            'maximalist': 'rich, detailed, layered design'
        }
        
        mood_modifiers = {
            'professional': 'corporate, trustworthy, authoritative',
            'friendly': 'warm, approachable, welcoming',
            'energetic': 'dynamic, vibrant, exciting',
            'calm': 'peaceful, serene, tranquil',
            'playful': 'fun, creative, whimsical'
        }
        
        style_mod = style_modifiers.get(style, '')
        mood_mod = mood_modifiers.get(mood, '')
        
        enhanced_prompt = f"{base_prompt}, {style_mod}, {mood_mod}, high quality, marketing material"
        
        # Crear variaciones del prompt
        variations = [
            enhanced_prompt,
            f"{enhanced_prompt}, close-up view",
            f"{enhanced_prompt}, wide angle view",
            f"{enhanced_prompt}, aerial perspective"
        ]
        
        return variations
    
    def generate_graphics(self, brief, style_preferences):
        """Generar grï¿½ï¿½ficos y elementos visuales"""
        graphics = {
            'logos': self.generate_logo_concepts(brief),
            'icons': self.generate_icon_set(brief),
            'infographics': self.generate_infographic_concepts(brief),
            'charts': self.generate_chart_templates(brief)
        }
        return graphics
    
    def generate_logo_concepts(self, brief):
        """Generar conceptos de logo"""
        brand_name = brief.get('brand_name', 'Brand')
        industry = brief.get('industry', 'general')
        
        logo_concepts = []
        
        # Conceptos basados en industria
        industry_concepts = {
            'technology': ['geometric', 'futuristic', 'minimalist'],
            'healthcare': ['trustworthy', 'clean', 'professional'],
            'finance': ['stable', 'professional', 'traditional'],
            'creative': ['artistic', 'dynamic', 'innovative'],
            'retail': ['friendly', 'approachable', 'vibrant']
        }
        
        concepts = industry_concepts.get(industry, ['modern', 'clean', 'professional'])
        
        for concept in concepts:
            logo_concept = {
                'name': f"{brand_name} - {concept.title()}",
                'style': concept,
                'description': f"Logo concept featuring {concept} design elements",
                'color_scheme': self.get_color_scheme_for_concept(concept),
                'typography': self.get_typography_for_concept(concept)
            }
            logo_concepts.append(logo_concept)
        
        return logo_concepts
    
    def generate_infographic_concepts(self, brief):
        """Generar conceptos de infografï¿½ï¿½a"""
        data_points = brief.get('data_points', [])
        topic = brief.get('topic', 'General Information')
        
        infographic_concepts = []
        
        for i, data_point in enumerate(data_points):
            concept = {
                'title': f"{topic} - Data Point {i+1}",
                'data': data_point,
                'layout': self.suggest_infographic_layout(data_point),
                'visual_elements': self.suggest_visual_elements(data_point),
                'color_scheme': self.get_color_scheme_for_data(data_point)
            }
            infographic_concepts.append(concept)
        
        return infographic_concepts
    
    def create_video_content_strategy(self, brief, budget, timeline):
        """Crear estrategia de contenido de video"""
        strategy = {
            'video_types': self.recommend_video_types(brief),
            'production_approach': self.recommend_production_approach(budget),
            'distribution_strategy': self.create_distribution_strategy(brief),
            'success_metrics': self.define_video_metrics(brief)
        }
        
        return strategy
    
    def recommend_video_types(self, brief):
        """Recomendar tipos de video"""
        objectives = brief.get('objectives', [])
        target_audience = brief.get('target_audience', 'general')
        
        video_recommendations = []
        
        if 'awareness' in objectives:
            video_recommendations.extend([
                'Brand Story Video',
                'Product Demo Video',
                'Behind-the-Scenes Video',
                'Educational Content Video'
            ])
        
        if 'engagement' in objectives:
            video_recommendations.extend([
                'Interactive Video',
                'User-Generated Content',
                'Live Streaming',
                'Social Media Stories'
            ])
        
        if 'conversion' in objectives:
            video_recommendations.extend([
                'Product Showcase Video',
                'Testimonial Video',
                'How-to Video',
                'Comparison Video'
            ])
        
        return video_recommendations
    
    def create_audio_content_strategy(self, brief):
        """Crear estrategia de contenido de audio"""
        strategy = {
            'podcast_episodes': self.plan_podcast_content(brief),
            'audio_ads': self.create_audio_ad_concepts(brief),
            'voice_optimization': self.optimize_for_voice(brief),
            'audio_branding': self.create_audio_branding(brief)
        }
        
        return strategy
    
    def plan_podcast_content(self, brief):
        """Planificar contenido de podcast"""
        topics = brief.get('topics', [])
        format_preferences = brief.get('format', 'interview')
        
        episodes = []
        
        for i, topic in enumerate(topics):
            episode = {
                'title': f"Episode {i+1}: {topic}",
                'topic': topic,
                'format': format_preferences,
                'duration': self.suggest_episode_duration(topic),
                'guests': self.suggest_guests(topic),
                'key_points': self.outline_key_points(topic)
            }
            episodes.append(episode)
        
        return episodes

# Uso del sistema creativo
creative_ai = CreativeAIMarketing()
brief = {
    'description': 'Modern tech startup launching new app',
    'brand_name': 'TechFlow',
    'industry': 'technology',
    'objectives': ['awareness', 'engagement'],
    'target_audience': 'tech professionals'
}
style_preferences = {
    'style': 'modern',
    'mood': 'professional',
    'colors': 'blue and white'
}
content = creative_ai.generate_visual_content(brief, style_preferences)
```

## ï¿½x ï¿½ MARKETING Mï¿½ VIL AVANZADO CON IA

### **Sistema de Personalizaciï¿½ï¿½n Mï¿½ï¿½vil**
```python
import geopy
from geopy.distance import geodesic
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class MobileMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.user_profiles = {}
        self.location_data = {}
        self.behavior_patterns = {}
    
    def create_mobile_user_profile(self, user_id, device_data, location_data, behavior_data):
        """Crear perfil de usuario mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        profile = {
            'user_id': user_id,
            'device_info': self.analyze_device_info(device_data),
            'location_profile': self.analyze_location_patterns(location_data),
            'behavior_profile': self.analyze_behavior_patterns(behavior_data),
            'preferences': self.infer_preferences(device_data, location_data, behavior_data),
            'engagement_score': self.calculate_engagement_score(behavior_data),
            'conversion_probability': self.calculate_conversion_probability(behavior_data)
        }
        
        self.user_profiles[user_id] = profile
        return profile
    
    def analyze_device_info(self, device_data):
        """Analizar informaciï¿½ï¿½n del dispositivo"""
        device_analysis = {
            'device_type': device_data.get('device_type', 'unknown'),
            'os_version': device_data.get('os_version', 'unknown'),
            'screen_size': device_data.get('screen_size', 'unknown'),
            'app_usage_pattern': self.analyze_app_usage(device_data.get('installed_apps', [])),
            'performance_level': self.assess_device_performance(device_data)
        }
        return device_analysis
    
    def analyze_location_patterns(self, location_data):
        """Analizar patrones de ubicaciï¿½ï¿½n"""
        if not location_data:
            return {}
        
        locations = pd.DataFrame(location_data)
        
        analysis = {
            'home_location': self.find_home_location(locations),
            'work_location': self.find_work_location(locations),
            'frequent_places': self.find_frequent_places(locations),
            'travel_patterns': self.analyze_travel_patterns(locations),
            'geofence_opportunities': self.identify_geofence_opportunities(locations)
        }
        
        return analysis
    
    def find_home_location(self, locations_df):
        """Encontrar ubicaciï¿½ï¿½n del hogar"""
        # Buscar ubicaciï¿½ï¿½n mï¿½ï¿½s frecuente durante la noche
        night_locations = locations_df[
            (locations_df['hour'] >= 22) | (locations_df['hour'] <= 6)
        ]
        
        if len(night_locations) > 0:
            home_lat = night_locations['latitude'].mode().iloc[0]
            home_lon = night_locations['longitude'].mode().iloc[0]
            return {'latitude': home_lat, 'longitude': home_lon}
        
        return None
    
    def find_work_location(self, locations_df):
        """Encontrar ubicaciï¿½ï¿½n del trabajo"""
        # Buscar ubicaciï¿½ï¿½n mï¿½ï¿½s frecuente durante horas laborales
        work_locations = locations_df[
            (locations_df['hour'] >= 9) & (locations_df['hour'] <= 17)
        ]
        
        if len(work_locations) > 0:
            work_lat = work_locations['latitude'].mode().iloc[0]
            work_lon = work_locations['longitude'].mode().iloc[0]
            return {'latitude': work_lat, 'longitude': work_lon}
        
        return None
    
    def identify_geofence_opportunities(self, locations_df):
        """Identificar oportunidades de geofencing"""
        opportunities = []
        
        # Buscar ubicaciones frecuentes que podrï¿½ï¿½an ser tiendas
        frequent_locations = locations_df.groupby(['latitude', 'longitude']).size().reset_index(name='count')
        frequent_locations = frequent_locations[frequent_locations['count'] >= 3]
        
        for _, location in frequent_locations.iterrows():
            opportunity = {
                'latitude': location['latitude'],
                'longitude': location['longitude'],
                'visit_frequency': location['count'],
                'geofence_radius': 100,  # metros
                'recommended_actions': self.recommend_geofence_actions(location['count'])
            }
            opportunities.append(opportunity)
        
        return opportunities
    
    def recommend_geofence_actions(self, visit_frequency):
        """Recomendar acciones de geofencing"""
        if visit_frequency >= 10:
            return ['push_notification', 'special_offer', 'loyalty_reward']
        elif visit_frequency >= 5:
            return ['push_notification', 'product_recommendation']
        else:
            return ['welcome_message', 'first_time_offer']
    
    def create_mobile_campaign_strategy(self, target_audience, objectives, budget):
        """Crear estrategia de campaï¿½ï¿½a mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        strategy = {
            'channel_strategy': self.plan_mobile_channels(target_audience),
            'content_strategy': self.plan_mobile_content(target_audience, objectives),
            'timing_strategy': self.plan_mobile_timing(target_audience),
            'personalization_strategy': self.plan_personalization(target_audience),
            'budget_allocation': self.allocate_mobile_budget(budget, target_audience)
        }
        
        return strategy
    
    def plan_mobile_channels(self, target_audience):
        """Planificar canales mï¿½ï¿½viles"""
        channels = {
            'in_app_advertising': {
                'priority': 'high',
                'reason': 'High engagement and targeting precision',
                'budget_percentage': 0.4
            },
            'push_notifications': {
                'priority': 'high',
                'reason': 'Direct communication channel',
                'budget_percentage': 0.2
            },
            'social_media_mobile': {
                'priority': 'medium',
                'reason': 'High reach and engagement',
                'budget_percentage': 0.25
            },
            'mobile_search': {
                'priority': 'medium',
                'reason': 'Intent-based targeting',
                'budget_percentage': 0.15
            }
        }
        
        return channels
    
    def plan_mobile_content(self, target_audience, objectives):
        """Planificar contenido mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        content_strategy = {
            'visual_content': self.plan_visual_content(target_audience),
            'interactive_content': self.plan_interactive_content(target_audience),
            'video_content': self.plan_mobile_video(target_audience),
            'audio_content': self.plan_mobile_audio(target_audience)
        }
        
        return content_strategy
    
    def plan_visual_content(self, target_audience):
        """Planificar contenido visual mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        visual_strategy = {
            'image_sizes': ['1080x1080', '1080x1920', '1080x1350'],  # Instagram, Stories, Feed
            'design_principles': [
                'Mobile-first design',
                'Thumb-friendly interactions',
                'High contrast for small screens',
                'Fast loading optimization'
            ],
            'content_types': [
                'Product showcase images',
                'Lifestyle photography',
                'Infographic content',
                'User-generated content'
            ]
        }
        
        return visual_strategy
    
    def optimize_for_mobile_performance(self, content, device_info):
        """Optimizar contenido para rendimiento mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        optimizations = {
            'image_optimization': self.optimize_images_for_mobile(content.get('images', [])),
            'loading_optimization': self.optimize_loading_speed(content, device_info),
            'battery_optimization': self.optimize_for_battery_usage(content),
            'data_usage_optimization': self.optimize_data_usage(content)
        }
        
        return optimizations
    
    def optimize_images_for_mobile(self, images):
        """Optimizar imï¿½ï¿½genes para mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        optimized_images = []
        
        for image in images:
            optimized = {
                'original_url': image.get('url'),
                'mobile_url': self.create_mobile_image_url(image.get('url')),
                'compression_level': 'high',
                'format': 'WebP',
                'max_width': 1080,
                'max_height': 1920,
                'quality': 85
            }
            optimized_images.append(optimized)
        
        return optimized_images
    
    def create_mobile_image_url(self, original_url):
        """Crear URL de imagen optimizada para mï¿½ï¿½vil"""
        # En implementaciï¿½ï¿½n real, usar servicio de optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de imï¿½ï¿½genes
        return f"{original_url}?w=1080&h=1920&q=85&f=webp"

# Uso del sistema mï¿½ï¿½vil
mobile_ai = MobileMarketingAI()
device_data = {
    'device_type': 'smartphone',
    'os_version': 'iOS 17.0',
    'screen_size': '6.1 inch',
    'installed_apps': ['Instagram', 'TikTok', 'WhatsApp', 'Spotify']
}
location_data = [
    {'latitude': 40.7128, 'longitude': -74.0060, 'timestamp': '2024-01-01 09:00:00', 'hour': 9},
    {'latitude': 40.7128, 'longitude': -74.0060, 'timestamp': '2024-01-01 18:00:00', 'hour': 18}
]
behavior_data = {
    'app_usage_time': 120,  # minutos por dï¿½ï¿½a
    'purchase_history': ['product_a', 'product_b'],
    'engagement_actions': ['like', 'share', 'comment']
}
profile = mobile_ai.create_mobile_user_profile('user_123', device_data, location_data, behavior_data)
```

## ï¿½x   PRIVACIDAD Y ï¿½0 TICA EN IA MARKETING

### **Framework de ï¿½0 tica en IA**
```python
import hashlib
import json
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class AIEthicsFramework:
    def __init__(self):
        self.privacy_principles = {
            'transparency': 'Los usuarios deben entender cï¿½ï¿½mo se usan sus datos',
            'consent': 'Los usuarios deben dar consentimiento explï¿½ï¿½cito',
            'purpose_limitation': 'Los datos solo se usan para el propï¿½ï¿½sito declarado',
            'data_minimization': 'Solo se recopilan datos necesarios',
            'accuracy': 'Los datos deben ser precisos y actualizados',
            'security': 'Los datos deben estar protegidos',
            'accountability': 'Las organizaciones son responsables del uso de datos'
        }
        self.ethical_guidelines = {}
    
    def assess_data_privacy_compliance(self, data_collection_practices):
        """Evaluar cumplimiento de privacidad de datos"""
        compliance_score = 0
        total_checks = 0
        
        # Verificar transparencia
        transparency_score = self.check_transparency(data_collection_practices)
        compliance_score += transparency_score
        total_checks += 1
        
        # Verificar consentimiento
        consent_score = self.check_consent_management(data_collection_practices)
        compliance_score += consent_score
        total_checks += 1
        
        # Verificar minimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de datos
        minimization_score = self.check_data_minimization(data_collection_practices)
        compliance_score += minimization_score
        total_checks += 1
        
        # Verificar seguridad
        security_score = self.check_data_security(data_collection_practices)
        compliance_score += security_score
        total_checks += 1
        
        overall_score = compliance_score / total_checks
        
        return {
            'overall_score': overall_score,
            'compliance_level': self.get_compliance_level(overall_score),
            'recommendations': self.generate_privacy_recommendations(overall_score),
            'detailed_scores': {
                'transparency': transparency_score,
                'consent': consent_score,
                'minimization': minimization_score,
                'security': security_score
            }
        }
    
    def check_transparency(self, practices):
        """Verificar transparencia en el uso de datos"""
        score = 0
        
        # Verificar si hay polï¿½ï¿½tica de privacidad clara
        if practices.get('privacy_policy_exists', False):
            score += 0.25
        
        # Verificar si se explica el uso de IA
        if practices.get('ai_usage_explained', False):
            score += 0.25
        
        # Verificar si se explican los algoritmos
        if practices.get('algorithms_explained', False):
            score += 0.25
        
        # Verificar si se explican las decisiones automatizadas
        if practices.get('automated_decisions_explained', False):
            score += 0.25
        
        return score
    
    def check_consent_management(self, practices):
        """Verificar gestiï¿½ï¿½n de consentimiento"""
        score = 0
        
        # Verificar si se obtiene consentimiento explï¿½ï¿½cito
        if practices.get('explicit_consent', False):
            score += 0.3
        
        # Verificar si se puede retirar el consentimiento
        if practices.get('consent_withdrawal', False):
            score += 0.3
        
        # Verificar si se documenta el consentimiento
        if practices.get('consent_documentation', False):
            score += 0.2
        
        # Verificar si se actualiza el consentimiento
        if practices.get('consent_updates', False):
            score += 0.2
        
        return score
    
    def create_ethical_ai_guidelines(self, organization_type, industry):
        """Crear pautas ï¿½ï¿½ticas de IA para la organizaciï¿½ï¿½n"""
        guidelines = {
            'data_collection': self.create_data_collection_guidelines(organization_type, industry),
            'algorithm_development': self.create_algorithm_guidelines(organization_type, industry),
            'decision_making': self.create_decision_making_guidelines(organization_type, industry),
            'monitoring': self.create_monitoring_guidelines(organization_type, industry)
        }
        
        return guidelines
    
    def create_data_collection_guidelines(self, organization_type, industry):
        """Crear pautas para recopilaciï¿½ï¿½n de datos"""
        guidelines = {
            'principles': [
                'Solo recopilar datos necesarios para el propï¿½ï¿½sito declarado',
                'Obtener consentimiento explï¿½ï¿½cito antes de recopilar datos',
                'Proporcionar informaciï¿½ï¿½n clara sobre el uso de datos',
                'Permitir a los usuarios acceder, corregir y eliminar sus datos'
            ],
            'technical_requirements': [
                'Implementar cifrado de extremo a extremo',
                'Usar tï¿½ï¿½cnicas de anonimizaciï¿½ï¿½n cuando sea posible',
                'Implementar controles de acceso basados en roles',
                'Realizar auditorï¿½ï¿½as regulares de seguridad'
            ],
            'legal_requirements': [
                'Cumplir con GDPR, CCPA y otras regulaciones aplicables',
                'Mantener registros de procesamiento de datos',
                'Implementar procedimientos de notificaciï¿½ï¿½n de violaciones',
                'Designar un oficial de protecciï¿½ï¿½n de datos si es necesario'
            ]
        }
        
        return guidelines
    
    def create_algorithm_guidelines(self, organization_type, industry):
        """Crear pautas para desarrollo de algoritmos"""
        guidelines = {
            'fairness': [
                'Evitar sesgos en los datos de entrenamiento',
                'Probar algoritmos con datos diversos',
                'Implementar mï¿½ï¿½tricas de equidad',
                'Revisar regularmente los resultados por demografï¿½ï¿½a'
            ],
            'transparency': [
                'Documentar el proceso de desarrollo',
                'Explicar las decisiones del algoritmo',
                'Proporcionar interpretabilidad cuando sea posible',
                'Mantener registros de versiones y cambios'
            ],
            'accountability': [
                'Asignar responsabilidades claras',
                'Implementar procesos de revisiï¿½ï¿½n',
                'Establecer canales de apelaciï¿½ï¿½n',
                'Mantener registros de decisiones'
            ]
        }
        
        return guidelines
    
    def implement_privacy_by_design(self, system_architecture):
        """Implementar privacidad por diseï¿½ï¿½o"""
        privacy_features = {
            'data_minimization': self.implement_data_minimization(system_architecture),
            'purpose_limitation': self.implement_purpose_limitation(system_architecture),
            'storage_limitation': self.implement_storage_limitation(system_architecture),
            'transparency': self.implement_transparency_features(system_architecture),
            'user_control': self.implement_user_control_features(system_architecture)
        }
        
        return privacy_features
    
    def implement_data_minimization(self, architecture):
        """Implementar minimizaciï¿½ï¿½n de datos"""
        features = {
            'data_classification': 'Clasificar datos por sensibilidad',
            'retention_policies': 'Implementar polï¿½ï¿½ticas de retenciï¿½ï¿½n automï¿½ï¿½ticas',
            'anonymization': 'Anonimizar datos cuando sea posible',
            'pseudonymization': 'Usar pseudï¿½ï¿½nimos para datos personales',
            'data_masking': 'Enmascarar datos sensibles en logs'
        }
        
        return features
    
    def create_ai_audit_framework(self):
        """Crear framework de auditorï¿½ï¿½a de IA"""
        audit_framework = {
            'data_audit': {
                'frequency': 'quarterly',
                'scope': 'All data collection and processing activities',
                'methodology': 'Automated scanning + manual review',
                'deliverables': ['Data inventory', 'Compliance report', 'Risk assessment']
            },
            'algorithm_audit': {
                'frequency': 'bi-annually',
                'scope': 'All AI models and algorithms',
                'methodology': 'Bias testing + performance review',
                'deliverables': ['Bias report', 'Performance metrics', 'Recommendations']
            },
            'privacy_audit': {
                'frequency': 'annually',
                'scope': 'Privacy compliance and data protection',
                'methodology': 'Third-party assessment',
                'deliverables': ['Privacy impact assessment', 'Compliance certificate', 'Action plan']
            }
        }
        
        return audit_framework
    
    def generate_ethical_ai_report(self, organization_data):
        """Generar reporte de ï¿½ï¿½tica en IA"""
        report = {
            'executive_summary': self.create_executive_summary(organization_data),
            'compliance_status': self.assess_data_privacy_compliance(organization_data),
            'risk_assessment': self.perform_risk_assessment(organization_data),
            'recommendations': self.generate_ethical_recommendations(organization_data),
            'action_plan': self.create_ethical_action_plan(organization_data)
        }
        
        return report
    
    def create_executive_summary(self, data):
        """Crear resumen ejecutivo"""
        summary = {
            'overall_status': 'Compliance Level: High',
            'key_findings': [
                'Strong data protection measures in place',
                'Good transparency practices',
                'Areas for improvement in algorithm explainability'
            ],
            'priority_actions': [
                'Implement algorithm explainability features',
                'Enhance user consent management',
                'Conduct regular bias testing'
            ]
        }
        
        return summary

# Uso del framework ï¿½ï¿½tico
ethics_framework = AIEthicsFramework()
practices = {
    'privacy_policy_exists': True,
    'ai_usage_explained': True,
    'algorithms_explained': False,
    'automated_decisions_explained': True,
    'explicit_consent': True,
    'consent_withdrawal': True,
    'consent_documentation': True,
    'consent_updates': False
}
compliance = ethics_framework.assess_data_privacy_compliance(practices)
guidelines = ethics_framework.create_ethical_ai_guidelines('technology', 'marketing')
```

## ï¿½xaï¿½  INNOVACIï¿½ N Y FUTURO DE LA IA EN MARKETING

### **Tendencias Emergentes 2025-2030**

#### **1. Marketing Cuï¿½ï¿½ntico**
```python
import numpy as np
from qiskit import QuantumCircuit, transpile, assemble, Aer, execute

class QuantumMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.quantum_simulator = Aer.get_backend('qasm_simulator')
    
    def quantum_optimization(self, marketing_problems):
        """Optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n cuï¿½ï¿½ntica para problemas de marketing"""
        # Crear circuito cuï¿½ï¿½ntico para optimizaciï¿½ï¿½n
        qc = QuantumCircuit(3, 3)
        
        # Aplicar superposiciï¿½ï¿½n cuï¿½ï¿½ntica
        qc.h(0)
        qc.h(1)
        qc.h(2)
        
        # Entrelazamiento cuï¿½ï¿½ntico para correlaciones
        qc.cx(0, 1)
        qc.cx(1, 2)
        
        # Mediciï¿½ï¿½n
        qc.measure_all()
        
        # Ejecutar en simulador
        job = execute(qc, self.quantum_simulator, shots=1024)
        result = job.result()
        counts = result.get_counts(qc)
        
        return self.interpret_quantum_results(counts, marketing_problems)
    
    def quantum_segmentation(self, customer_data):
        """Segmentaciï¿½ï¿½n cuï¿½ï¿½ntica de clientes"""
        # Algoritmo cuï¿½ï¿½ntico para segmentaciï¿½ï¿½n
        segments = self.quantum_clustering(customer_data)
        return segments
    
    def quantum_prediction(self, historical_data):
        """Predicciï¿½ï¿½n cuï¿½ï¿½ntica de tendencias"""
        # Algoritmo cuï¿½ï¿½ntico para predicciï¿½ï¿½n
        predictions = self.quantum_forecasting(historical_data)
        return predictions

# Uso del marketing cuï¿½ï¿½ntico
quantum_marketing = QuantumMarketingAI()
problems = ['budget_allocation', 'channel_optimization', 'audience_targeting']
quantum_solution = quantum_marketing.quantum_optimization(problems)
```

#### **2. Realidad Extendida (XR) en Marketing**
```python
import cv2
import numpy as np
from sklearn.cluster import KMeans

class XRMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.ar_models = {}
        self.vr_environments = {}
        self.mr_interfaces = {}
    
    def create_ar_experience(self, product_data, user_preferences):
        """Crear experiencia de realidad aumentada"""
        ar_experience = {
            'product_overlay': self.generate_product_overlay(product_data),
            'interactive_elements': self.create_interactive_elements(user_preferences),
            'spatial_mapping': self.create_spatial_mapping(),
            'gesture_recognition': self.setup_gesture_recognition(),
            'voice_commands': self.setup_voice_commands()
        }
        return ar_experience
    
    def generate_product_overlay(self, product_data):
        """Generar overlay de producto en AR"""
        overlay = {
            '3d_model': product_data.get('3d_model_url'),
            'animations': self.create_product_animations(product_data),
            'interactions': self.define_product_interactions(product_data),
            'measurements': self.calculate_product_measurements(product_data)
        }
        return overlay
    
    def create_vr_showroom(self, products, brand_identity):
        """Crear showroom virtual"""
        showroom = {
            'environment': self.design_vr_environment(brand_identity),
            'product_displays': self.arrange_product_displays(products),
            'navigation': self.create_vr_navigation(),
            'interactions': self.define_vr_interactions(products),
            'social_features': self.add_social_features()
        }
        return showroom
    
    def setup_mixed_reality(self, physical_space, digital_elements):
        """Configurar realidad mixta"""
        mr_setup = {
            'spatial_anchors': self.create_spatial_anchors(physical_space),
            'digital_objects': self.place_digital_objects(digital_elements),
            'collision_detection': self.setup_collision_detection(),
            'lighting_matching': self.match_lighting_conditions(),
            'occlusion_handling': self.handle_occlusion()
        }
        return mr_setup

# Uso del marketing XR
xr_marketing = XRMarketingAI()
product_data = {'name': 'Smart Watch', '3d_model_url': 'models/smartwatch.obj'}
ar_exp = xr_marketing.create_ar_experience(product_data, {'style': 'modern'})
```

#### **3. Marketing Consciente y Emocional**
```python
import tensorflow as tf
from tensorflow.keras.models import Sequential
from tensorflow.keras.layers import LSTM, Dense, Attention
import librosa
import cv2

class ConsciousMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.emotion_model = self.build_emotion_model()
        self.consciousness_model = self.build_consciousness_model()
    
    def build_emotion_model(self):
        """Construir modelo de reconocimiento de emociones"""
        model = Sequential([
            LSTM(128, return_sequences=True, input_shape=(None, 256)),
            Attention(),
            LSTM(64),
            Dense(32, activation='relu'),
            Dense(7, activation='softmax')  # 7 emociones bï¿½ï¿½sicas
        ])
        return model
    
    def analyze_emotional_state(self, user_data):
        """Analizar estado emocional del usuario"""
        emotions = {
            'facial_emotion': self.analyze_facial_emotion(user_data.get('face_image')),
            'voice_emotion': self.analyze_voice_emotion(user_data.get('audio_data')),
            'text_emotion': self.analyze_text_emotion(user_data.get('text_data')),
            'behavioral_emotion': self.analyze_behavioral_emotion(user_data.get('behavior_data'))
        }
        
        # Combinar emociones para estado general
        overall_emotion = self.combine_emotions(emotions)
        return overall_emotion
    
    def create_conscious_marketing_message(self, user_emotion, product_info, brand_values):
        """Crear mensaje de marketing consciente"""
        message = {
            'tone': self.select_appropriate_tone(user_emotion),
            'content': self.craft_conscious_content(user_emotion, product_info, brand_values),
            'delivery_method': self.choose_delivery_method(user_emotion),
            'timing': self.optimize_timing(user_emotion),
            'follow_up': self.plan_follow_up(user_emotion)
        }
        return message
    
    def select_appropriate_tone(self, emotion):
        """Seleccionar tono apropiado segï¿½ï¿½n emociï¿½ï¿½n"""
        tone_mapping = {
            'happy': 'celebratory',
            'sad': 'empathetic',
            'angry': 'calming',
            'fearful': 'reassuring',
            'surprised': 'explanatory',
            'disgusted': 'reframing',
            'neutral': 'informative'
        }
        return tone_mapping.get(emotion, 'neutral')
    
    def craft_conscious_content(self, emotion, product_info, brand_values):
        """Crear contenido consciente"""
        content = {
            'headline': self.create_emotion_aware_headline(emotion, product_info),
            'body': self.write_emotion_resonant_body(emotion, product_info, brand_values),
            'call_to_action': self.create_emotion_appropriate_cta(emotion),
            'visual_elements': self.select_emotion_matching_visuals(emotion)
        }
        return content

# Uso del marketing consciente
conscious_marketing = ConsciousMarketingAI()
user_data = {
    'face_image': 'path/to/face.jpg',
    'audio_data': 'path/to/audio.wav',
    'text_data': 'I love this product!',
    'behavior_data': {'purchase_history': [], 'browsing_time': 300}
}
emotion = conscious_marketing.analyze_emotional_state(user_data)
```

## ï¿½xï¿½ï¿½ NEUROMARKETING Y IA

### **Sistema de Neuromarketing Avanzado**
```python
import numpy as np
from scipy import signal
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

class NeuromarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.eeg_processor = EEGProcessor()
        self.eye_tracker = EyeTracker()
        self.facial_coder = FacialCoder()
        self.galvanic_skin = GalvanicSkinResponse()
    
    def analyze_brain_response(self, eeg_data, stimulus):
        """Analizar respuesta cerebral a estï¿½ï¿½mulos"""
        # Procesar datos EEG
        processed_eeg = self.eeg_processor.process(eeg_data)
        
        # Extraer caracterï¿½ï¿½sticas relevantes
        features = {
            'alpha_power': self.extract_alpha_power(processed_eeg),
            'beta_power': self.extract_beta_power(processed_eeg),
            'theta_power': self.extract_theta_power(processed_eeg),
            'gamma_power': self.extract_gamma_power(processed_eeg),
            'attention_level': self.calculate_attention_level(processed_eeg),
            'emotional_arousal': self.calculate_emotional_arousal(processed_eeg)
        }
        
        return features
    
    def analyze_eye_movement(self, eye_tracking_data, visual_stimulus):
        """Analizar movimiento ocular"""
        eye_analysis = {
            'fixation_points': self.identify_fixation_points(eye_tracking_data),
            'saccade_patterns': self.analyze_saccade_patterns(eye_tracking_data),
            'heatmap': self.generate_heatmap(eye_tracking_data, visual_stimulus),
            'attention_areas': self.identify_attention_areas(eye_tracking_data),
            'reading_pattern': self.analyze_reading_pattern(eye_tracking_data)
        }
        
        return eye_analysis
    
    def analyze_facial_expressions(self, facial_data):
        """Analizar expresiones faciales"""
        expressions = {
            'emotions': self.detect_emotions(facial_data),
            'micro_expressions': self.detect_micro_expressions(facial_data),
            'valence': self.calculate_valence(facial_data),
            'arousal': self.calculate_arousal(facial_data),
            'dominance': self.calculate_dominance(facial_data)
        }
        
        return expressions
    
    def analyze_physiological_response(self, physiological_data):
        """Analizar respuesta fisiolï¿½ï¿½gica"""
        response = {
            'heart_rate': self.analyze_heart_rate(physiological_data.get('heart_rate')),
            'skin_conductance': self.analyze_skin_conductance(physiological_data.get('gsr')),
            'muscle_tension': self.analyze_muscle_tension(physiological_data.get('emg')),
            'respiration': self.analyze_respiration(physiological_data.get('respiration'))
        }
        
        return response
    
    def create_neuromarketing_insights(self, all_data):
        """Crear insights de neuromarketing"""
        insights = {
            'attention_score': self.calculate_attention_score(all_data),
            'emotional_impact': self.calculate_emotional_impact(all_data),
            'memory_encoding': self.assess_memory_encoding(all_data),
            'purchase_intent': self.predict_purchase_intent(all_data),
            'brand_recall': self.predict_brand_recall(all_data),
            'recommendations': self.generate_neuromarketing_recommendations(all_data)
        }
        
        return insights
    
    def optimize_marketing_content(self, neuromarketing_insights, content):
        """Optimizar contenido basado en neuromarketing"""
        optimized_content = {
            'visual_elements': self.optimize_visual_elements(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'text_content': self.optimize_text_content(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'layout': self.optimize_layout(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'colors': self.optimize_colors(neuromarketing_insights, content),
            'timing': self.optimize_timing(neuromarketing_insights, content)
        }
        
        return optimized_content

class EEGProcessor:
    def process(self, eeg_data):
        """Procesar datos EEG"""
        # Filtrado de ruido
        filtered_data = self.filter_noise(eeg_data)
        
        # Extracciï¿½ï¿½n de caracterï¿½ï¿½sticas
        features = self.extract_features(filtered_data)
        
        return features
    
    def filter_noise(self, data):
        """Filtrar ruido de los datos EEG"""
        # Aplicar filtro de banda
        filtered = signal.butter(4, [1, 40], btype='band', fs=256, output='sos')
        filtered_data = signal.sosfilt(filtered, data)
        return filtered_data
    
    def extract_features(self, data):
        """Extraer caracterï¿½ï¿½sticas de los datos EEG"""
        features = {
            'power_spectral_density': self.calculate_psd(data),
            'coherence': self.calculate_coherence(data),
            'phase_locking': self.calculate_phase_locking(data)
        }
        return features

# Uso del neuromarketing
neuromarketing = NeuromarketingAI()
eeg_data = np.random.randn(256, 1000)  # Datos de ejemplo
brain_response = neuromarketing.analyze_brain_response(eeg_data, 'ad_stimulus')
```

## ï¿½xRï¿½ SOSTENIBILIDAD Y MARKETING VERDE CON IA

### **Sistema de Marketing Sostenible**
```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class SustainableMarketingAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.carbon_footprint_calculator = CarbonFootprintCalculator()
        self.sustainability_metrics = SustainabilityMetrics()
        self.green_ai_optimizer = GreenAIOptimizer()
    
    def calculate_carbon_footprint(self, marketing_activities):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de actividades de marketing"""
        footprint = {
            'digital_ads': self.calculate_digital_ads_footprint(marketing_activities.get('digital_ads', [])),
            'email_campaigns': self.calculate_email_footprint(marketing_activities.get('emails', [])),
            'content_creation': self.calculate_content_footprint(marketing_activities.get('content', [])),
            'events': self.calculate_events_footprint(marketing_activities.get('events', [])),
            'packaging': self.calculate_packaging_footprint(marketing_activities.get('packaging', []))
        }
        
        total_footprint = sum(footprint.values())
        footprint['total'] = total_footprint
        footprint['equivalent'] = self.convert_to_equivalents(total_footprint)
        
        return footprint
    
    def calculate_digital_ads_footprint(self, digital_ads):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de anuncios digitales"""
        total_impressions = sum(ad.get('impressions', 0) for ad in digital_ads)
        total_clicks = sum(ad.get('clicks', 0) for ad in digital_ads)
        
        # Estimaciï¿½ï¿½n de CO2 por impresiï¿½ï¿½n y click
        co2_per_impression = 0.000001  # kg CO2
        co2_per_click = 0.00001  # kg CO2
        
        total_co2 = (total_impressions * co2_per_impression) + (total_clicks * co2_per_click)
        return total_co2
    
    def optimize_for_sustainability(self, marketing_strategy):
        """Optimizar estrategia de marketing para sostenibilidad"""
        optimized_strategy = {
            'channel_optimization': self.optimize_channels_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy),
            'content_optimization': self.optimize_content_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy),
            'timing_optimization': self.optimize_timing_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy),
            'targeting_optimization': self.optimize_targeting_for_sustainability(marketing_strategy)
        }
        
        return optimized_strategy
    
    def optimize_channels_for_sustainability(self, strategy):
        """Optimizar canales para sostenibilidad"""
        channel_sustainability = {
            'email': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000004, 'effectiveness': 0.8},
            'social_media': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000002, 'effectiveness': 0.6},
            'search_ads': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000001, 'effectiveness': 0.9},
            'display_ads': {'co2_per_contact': 0.000003, 'effectiveness': 0.4},
            'print_media': {'co2_per_contact': 0.01, 'effectiveness': 0.7}
        }
        
        # Seleccionar canales mï¿½ï¿½s sostenibles
        sustainable_channels = []
        for channel, metrics in channel_sustainability.items():
            sustainability_score = metrics['effectiveness'] / metrics['co2_per_contact']
            if sustainability_score > 1000:  # Umbral de sostenibilidad
                sustainable_channels.append({
                    'channel': channel,
                    'sustainability_score': sustainability_score,
                    'recommended_budget_share': self.calculate_budget_share(sustainability_score)
                })
        
        return sustainable_channels
    
    def create_sustainability_report(self, marketing_activities, period):
        """Crear reporte de sostenibilidad"""
        report = {
            'period': period,
            'carbon_footprint': self.calculate_carbon_footprint(marketing_activities),
            'sustainability_goals': self.assess_sustainability_goals(marketing_activities),
            'improvements': self.identify_improvements(marketing_activities),
            'recommendations': self.generate_sustainability_recommendations(marketing_activities),
            'benchmarks': self.compare_with_benchmarks(marketing_activities)
        }
        
        return report
    
    def assess_sustainability_goals(self, activities):
        """Evaluar objetivos de sostenibilidad"""
        goals = {
            'carbon_neutral': self.assess_carbon_neutrality(activities),
            'waste_reduction': self.assess_waste_reduction(activities),
            'renewable_energy': self.assess_renewable_energy_usage(activities),
            'circular_economy': self.assess_circular_economy_practices(activities)
        }
        
        return goals
    
    def generate_sustainability_recommendations(self, activities):
        """Generar recomendaciones de sostenibilidad"""
        recommendations = []
        
        # Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de huella de carbono
        footprint = self.calculate_carbon_footprint(activities)
        if footprint['total'] > 1000:  # kg CO2
            recommendations.append({
                'priority': 'high',
                'category': 'carbon_reduction',
                'action': 'Implementar estrategias de marketing digital mï¿½ï¿½s eficientes',
                'potential_savings': '30-50% reducciï¿½ï¿½n en huella de carbono'
            })
        
        # Anï¿½ï¿½lisis de canales
        channel_analysis = self.analyze_channel_sustainability(activities)
        if channel_analysis['least_sustainable']:
            recommendations.append({
                'priority': 'medium',
                'category': 'channel_optimization',
                'action': f"Reducir uso de {channel_analysis['least_sustainable']}",
                'potential_savings': '20-40% reducciï¿½ï¿½n en emisiones'
            })
        
        return recommendations

class CarbonFootprintCalculator:
    def __init__(self):
        self.emission_factors = {
            'electricity': 0.5,  # kg CO2 per kWh
            'data_center': 0.3,  # kg CO2 per GB
            'transportation': 0.2,  # kg CO2 per km
            'paper': 0.8  # kg CO2 per kg
        }
    
    def calculate_activity_footprint(self, activity_type, activity_data):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de una actividad especï¿½ï¿½fica"""
        if activity_type == 'email_campaign':
            return self.calculate_email_footprint(activity_data)
        elif activity_type == 'digital_ad':
            return self.calculate_digital_ad_footprint(activity_data)
        elif activity_type == 'content_creation':
            return self.calculate_content_creation_footprint(activity_data)
        else:
            return 0
    
    def calculate_email_footprint(self, email_data):
        """Calcular huella de carbono de emails"""
        recipients = email_data.get('recipients', 0)
        email_size = email_data.get('size_mb', 0.1)
        
        # CO2 por email (aproximadamente 4g)
        co2_per_email = 0.004
        
        return recipients * co2_per_email

# Uso del marketing sostenible
sustainable_marketing = SustainableMarketingAI()
activities = {
    'digital_ads': [{'impressions': 1000000, 'clicks': 10000}],
    'emails': [{'recipients': 50000, 'size_mb': 0.1}],
    'content': [{'videos': 10, 'images': 50, 'articles': 20}]
}
footprint = sustainable_marketing.calculate_carbon_footprint(activities)
```
